            };
            var html = _.template(template)(translations).replace('@@link@@', '/cookiepolicy.aspx');
            $('body').prepend(html);
            var trackingEvent = {
                mixpanel: [{ name: 'Cookie Policy Alert Visible' }]
            }
            Skyscanner.Common.observer.publish('tracking-event', trackingEvent);
            Skyscanner.Common.observer.publish('cookie-policy-opened');
            Skyscanner.Api.localStorage.init('web').trySetValue('user.cookiePolicyShown', true, true);

            $('#cookie a.acknowledge').click(function (e) {
                e.stopPropagation();
                Skyscanner.Api.localStorage.init('web').trySetValue('user.cookiePolicyAcknowledged', true, true);
                $('#cookie').hide();
                Skyscanner.Common.observer.publish('cookie-policy-closed');
                return false;
            });    
        };
        $.ajax({
            url: src,
            success: onTranslationsLoaded,
            dataType: "script",
            cache: true
        });
    })();        
</script>
<script id="cookie-policy-template" type="text/template">
    <div id="cookie" class="fade clearfix">
        <div class="f-container">
            <p class="text">
                <%=ktxtCookiePolicyHeaderBar%>
            </p>
            <a href="#" class="acknowledge"><%=ktxtCookiePolicyHeaderBarOk%></a>
        </div>
    </div>
</script><iframe src="https://tpc.googlesyndication.com/safeframe/1-0-2/html/container.html" width="0" height="0" style="visibility: hidden !important; display: none !important; opacity: 0 !important;"></iframe>
